< Text>
By far one of the best parks for the kiddos. They've got an upgraded playground, volleyball court, soccer and football fields, softball field, skatepark, basketball courts and picnic area with BBQ grills. They no longer have working sinks in the picnic area and the drinking fountain doesn't work. Other than that, summer time is awesome with the kids. Just don't come out at night, its a little sketchy.< /Text>

< Review>
I was not at all satisfied with Stanley Steamer .  My appointment window was between 11am and 2 pm.  They arrived at 3:30 pm.  They did phone at 1:20 to say they would be late and I was grateful they did that.  But needless to say, the time delay messed up other plans.

< Text>
I did a little research looking for a tailor to get some pants hemmed. The Suit Co. came up with glowing reviews, and I decided to check them out as I needed a few pairs done asap. I sent an appointment request via Yelp and was told to just walk in. There was a wedding party in the store when we arrived. We were not greeted when we entered the store (no problem, being busy with customers is usually a good thing!) Finally had someone acknowledge us (about ten minutes later), then waited around some more before they were ready to assist.

We were there just to get some pants hemmed. Nothing fancy. We went into the fitting room to try on the pants, then came out expecting to get fitted. I was then told that they don't have time for us. We walked out and decided to take our business elsewhere.

After communicating with Abel (via Yelp), I was told that they don't take appointments and only work as a first come first serve basis. I'm baffled as to why a company that sells suits (and obviously caters to wedding parties) does not take appointments. I'm equally baffled at the lack of employees working the floor on a Sunday afternoon. It just does not seem efficient.<//Text>

Additional donations are optional as it keeps the museum open. There is also a lower level room which contains more Hardware and tools use during the time. <Text>This is a storage facility worth checking out. I found this place online and called the toll free number and spoke to Matt. He assisted me with renting a unit for my needs on their website. I got a great web rate for the unit. While we were on the call his computer went down, this resulted in my being charged twice for the deposit, but they were happy to credit my account once I provided proof of the mistake.

All of my questions were asked and there is no real catch to the low prices you see online. You do have to get insurance protection for your valuables and it is an additional cost, but probably worth it in the long run. It's for your protection and theirs. As I was getting of the phone with Matt at the call center, I got a call right away from Charlene, who welcomed me aboard and asked if I had additional questions and offered that I come in to take a look at the unit just to be sure it was what I was looking for.

Today, I went in to take care of the financials before I moved in and met Jerry the manager. He is very cool, calm and patient. He drove me around the cute little golf cart to show me the units and space. Place is very very clean, and even though my unit is upstairs, they have a freight elevator (it is working) and a dolly in case you don't have one available. While waiting to finalize my account the power went down twice (not their fault, men were working on the premises) and Jerry just tugged along and thanked me for my patience.

They have some of the best prices around, would be hard to beat them in such a great location in San Leandro and everyone is very friendly and accommodating and they let you know everything you need to know up front. The space is open every day and even late hours should you need to move stuff in or out after 7pm.

I would recommend them to anyone looking for great rates, fast friendly service and a clean, safe area to store your belongings.<//Text>< userid>

My whole experience with this location and it's staff has been wonderful.  I initially made my reservation online for a 5X10 space, thinking that it would be enough for the stuff that I had.  Once I made my reservation online, I immediately received a phone call from the Site Manager, Jerry.  He was very friendly and provided me with all the information I needed. I did run into a little bit of a snag, but the reps assisted me and I got my unit.

I think that the location of this facility is great for me, as I am still in transition to finding a new place to live and my things are centrally located. I feel secure knowing that my personal belongings are protected.  The facility is very secure with two gated entrances, security passcodes needed to get in and out of the facility, an onsite manager, and video surveillance.
